Kafka consumer group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java files in the group-coordinator module. The implementation includes three main group types with different state models:\\n\\n1. **Classic Group State Machine** (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.classic):\\n   - ClassicGroupState.java defines the state enum with 5 states: EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, and DEAD\\n   - Each state has defined valid previous states, forming a state transition graph\\n   - ClassicGroup.java implements the group class with the transitionTo() method for state transitions\\n   - The classic group joins follow the join-sync-rebalance protocol:\\n     * EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE (when join group received)\\n     * PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE (when all members joined or timeout)\\n     * COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE (when sync group received from leader)\\n     * STABLE → PREPARING_REBALANCE (on member failure, leave, or new join)\\n     * All states can → DEAD (on removal)\\n\\n2. **Modern Consumer Group State Machine** (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.consumer):\\n   - ConsumerGroup.java defines ConsumerGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n   - Uses a different rebalance protocol based on the KIP-848 consumer group protocol\\n   - Includes member-level state tracking via MemberState.java with states: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS\\n   - CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java manages the assignment state transitions for members\\n\\n3. **Share Group State Machine** (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.share):\\n   - ShareGroup.java defines ShareGroupState enum for managed share groups\\n   - Uses similar state machine patterns as consumer groups\\n\\n4. **Streams Group State Machine** (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.streams):\\n   - StreamsGroup.java defines StreamsGroupState enum for Kafka Streams applications\\n   - StreamsGroupMember.java and MemberState.java track member states\\n   - Includes topology-aware assignment via TargetAssignmentBuilder.java\\n\\n**Key Coordinator Classes**:\\n- GroupCoordinator.java: Interface defining the coordinator API for join, sync, and heartbeat operations\\n- GroupCoordinatorShard.java: The replicated state machine that manages all group metadata\\n- GroupMetadataManager.java: Contains handler methods classicGroupJoin(), classicGroupSync(), classicGroupHeartbeat(), and classicGroupLeave() that implement the request handling logic and state transitions\\n\\n**Request Flow**:\\n1. JoinGroup requests are handled by classicGroupJoin() which transitions groups through PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n2.
